---
  description: Use values without scaling and then convert them with ggplotly.
  function: scale_identity
  permalink: /ggplot2/Scales/scale_identity/
  layout: base
  language: ggplot2
  name: scale_identity
  reference: https://ggplot2.tidyverse.org/reference/
---


# Default plot

<pre class="mcode">
p <-    
 ggplot(luv_colours, aes(u, v)) +
  geom_point(aes(colour = col), size = 3) +
  scale_color_identity() +
  coord_equal()
  
plotly::ggplotly(p)
</pre>

# Setting a legend guide and label

<pre class="mcode">
df <- data.frame(
  x = 1:4,
  y = 1:4,
  colour = c("red", "green", "blue", "yellow")
)
p <-    
 ggplot(df, aes(x, y)) +
  geom_tile(aes(fill = colour)) +
  scale_fill_identity("trt", labels = letters[1:4], breaks = df$colour,
  guide = "legend")
  
plotly::ggplotly(p)
</pre>

# Scale data size


<pre class="mcode">
p <-    
 ggplot(mtcars, aes(mpg, wt)) +
  geom_point(aes(size = cyl))
  
plotly::ggplotly(p)
</pre>

<pre class="mcode">
p <-    
 ggplot(mtcars, aes(mpg, wt)) +
  geom_point(aes(size = cyl)) +
  scale_size_identity()
  
plotly::ggplotly(p)
